 Instead of imagining the formless God in the shape of human beings or beings, the facetling has been created in the shape of the world
 lingayat punarjanm main bhi vishwaas nahin karte hai
 Lingayats believe that there is only one life and anyone can make their life heaven and hell by their actions
 lingayat main shavon ko dafnane kii paramparalingayat parampara main antim sanskaar kii prakriya bhi alag he
 In Lingayat, bodies are buried
 lingayat parampara main mrityu ke baad shav ko nahalaakar bitha diya jaataa he
 The body is tied with the help of cloth or wood
 jab kisi lingayat kaa nidhan hota he to use sajaa-dhajaakar kursi par bithaaya jaataa he or phir kandhe par uthaaya jaataa he
 This is called aircraft tying
 kai jagahon par lingayaton ke alag kabristaan hote hai
 Basavanna's followers believe that Basavanna opposed the caste system and Vedic traditions
 unke andolan kaa aadhaar hi prachlit hindu vyavastha ke khilaaf tha
 They believe that the rules stated by the Ishta Linga and Lord Basaveshwara are completely different from Hinduism
 duusari taraf jo log lingayat kii hindu dharm se alag pahchaan kaa virodh karte hai, unka kahana he ki basavanna kaa andolan bhakthi andolan kii hi tarah tha
 His purpose was not to break away from the path of Hinduism
 bijepi kaa aarope- hinduon ko baantne kaa kaam kar rahi he congresslingayat samudaay ke bheetar lingayat ko hindu dharm se alag pahchaan dene kii baat samay-samay par doharaai jaati rahi he
 This demand has intensified in the last decade
 2011 kii janaganana ke dauraan, lingayat samooh ke kuch sanghathanon ne samudaay ke logon ko hindu dharm main register nahin hone ke liye campan bhi chalaae the
 The demand for an independent religious identity was made publicly for the first time in the Bidar Sabha
 is sabha main 50,000 se zyada log shaamil hue the
 The common belief is that Veerashaiva and Lingayat are the same people
 lekin lingayat logon kaa maananaa he ki virshaiv logon kaa astitv samaaj sudhaarak basavanna ke udai se bhi pehle se tha
 "basavanna rejected the Vedic ritual and tradition," says Mate Mahadevi, the first woman of the Lingayat community, Sadhvi and head of the Basava Dharma Peetha
 lekin virshaiv vedon kaa paalan karte hai
 They worship Shiva
 yahaan tak ki ve shiv kii murti puja bhi karte hai, spasht rup se basavanna kii avadharana ye nahin thi

 "karnataka main lagbhag 17 fisadi lingayat hai
 If they get religiously minority status then economically and socially backward people in the community will get the benefit of reservation
 pradesh ke kanoon mantri tibi jayachandra ne kaha, ''cabinet ne saaf kar diya he ki lingayat dharm ke logon ko aarakshan musalmaan, isai, jain, buddha or sikhon ke aarakshan kii keemat par nahin milegaa
 This benefit will not be available from the reservation provided to other religious and linguistic minorities
 ''karnataka main basavanna kaa vaaris banane kii hodalingayaton ko dharmik alpsankhyak kaa darja dilaane kii ladaai shuru karne vaale forum ke ek padaadhikari ne kaha, ''shuru main lingayaton ke bheetar daliton ne ek andolan shuru kiya tha
 This is because Dalits could not get the benefit of upper caste Lingayat people within the community
 ''is visheshgy samiti ke ek sadsy kaa kahana he ki lingayaton main 99 jatiyon main se aadhe se zyada dalit yaa pichhadi jatiyon se hai

" ham logon kii na keval hinduon se alag jati he balki ham dharmik rup se bhi alpsankhyak hai

 agar isko manyata milti he to bhagwatji ko chintaa karne kii jarurat nahin he kyonki ham hindu samskruti or viraasat ke khilaaf nahin hai
 "lingayats' political trends: Lingayats have traditionally been bjp's votebank

 iske baad lingayat samudaay ne phir se congress se duuri bana lee

 iske baad lingayaton ne bijepi ke bies yediurppa ko apana netaa chunaa

 is maheene rajya main do charnon main sthaneey nikaay ke chunaav hue

 The Central Investigation Agency (CBI) today faced harsh words when former West Bengal Governor Gopalkrishna Gandhi said that the CBI had gained notoriety as a 'weapon of government' and a 'dirty tricks department'
 sibiai ke atithi vaktaa ke taur par gandhi ne 15wein deepi kohli smriti vyaakhyaan main is jaanch agency ko soochna ke adhikaar kanoon (artiai) ke daayre main laane kii purajor pairvi kii or kaha ki ise ‘sansanikhej dhang’ se nahin, balki ‘behtareen dhang’ se swytt bananaa hoga
 Gandhi used strong words in the presence of CBI Director Ranjit Sinha and the entire senior officers
 unhone kaha, 'ise sarkaar ke eemaandaar sahyogi kii tarah nahin, balki hathiyaar ke taur par dekha jaataa he
 It is often referred to as DDT, which means not the colorless, tasteless, odorless insecticide (dichloro diphenyl trichloroethane), but the 'department of Dirty Tricks'
 ' Citing the issue of corruption, the 69-year-old Gandhi said that the CBI has a 'mixed image' in which everything is unpredictable and it has to change the image already created
 ‘indian institute of advasn studies’ (ies) ke adhyaksh gandhi ne kaha ki ‘artiai prashikshit’ janata sibiai ke badlaav kaa upkaran banane kii ummid karti he
 Gandhi said, 'CBI is wearing a garment of opacity and then it has jewelery of secrecy and finally a perfume of mystery
 ' unhone sibiai ko artiai ke daayre main laane kii pairvi karte hue kaha, 'yah bahut dayaneey he
 The CBI is investigating corruption and certain crime cases

 " During the presidential election campaign, Obama took on his rival Mitt Romney fiercely over the issue of his companies outsourcing American jobs
 obama ne kaha ki america naukariyon ko duusare deshon main bhejne waalon kii ovel offis (america raashtrapati kaa mukhya daftar) main koi jarurat nahin he
 Making this point an issue, Obama cited a report in 'the Washington Post'
 is report ke mutabik, romany kii companiyaan america naukariyon ko china or bharat jaise deshon main bhejne main sabase aage hai
 Speaking in an election campaign in Tampa, Florida, Obama said, "let me tell you, in the Oval Office we do not need a person to send jobs to other countries
" hamen ek aisa raashtrapati chahie jo america naukariyon or america utpaadan ke liye lade
 i want to do the same then i am contesting the presidential election for the second time
 ’‘da washington post’ main chapa lekh obama ke chunavi abhiyaan kaa hi ek hissaa tha
 In this article, Stephanie Cutter wrote that Mitt Romney's financial company, Ben Capital, has invested in a number of companies that allow American employees to get their jobs done in India and China at a low cost
 report kii lekhak kattar ne obama ke samarthakon ke liye ek video sandesh main kaha, ‘yah (romany) vahi aadmi he, jisane america naukariyon ko bachaane or china ke saamne datakar khadey rahane ke bade-bade vaayade kiye the
 But actually Romney and his colleagues have made a lot of money by sending American jobs overseas
 ’unhone kaha, ‘romany nijee kshetra ke saath-saath sarkari kshetra kaa kaam bhi outsource karwaane ke paksh main hai
 When he was governor of Massachusetts, he rejected the bill that prohibited companies doing government work from outside countries
 romany ne asal main sarkari kaamon ko bharat ke ek kol centre se karavaaya
 Comparing Romney to Obama, Cutter said, "president Obama has plans that will help millions of people get their jobs back and create small business jobs
" unki koshish he ki america naukariyaan desh se baahar naa jaaen
 For this, they are also fighting for tax waiver of companies that are bringing jobs back to the US
 ’obama ke varisht ranneetikaar david execroad ne bhi ek sammelan main is lekh ko aadhaar banaate hue kaha ki garvanar romany kii prishthbhumi kahin se bhi yah nahin darshaati ki ve america karmchaariyon or america naukariyon kaa paksh lenge

 Know what is call center call center is also called BPO

 Call centers are of two types
 1
 In bond call center 2
 Out bond kol centre 
 In bond call center: In this, customers call themselves with their problems
 Out bond kol centre:isamen customer care graahak ko kol karte hai
